                                            <span class="stat-caption typography-site-deep-dive-stat-subcopy">
                                                video playback on <br class="small"/>
                                                iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro &nbsp;Max

                                    <div class="headline dd-large-6 dd-medium-8 dd-small-12 dd-small-offset-1">
                                        <p class="eyebrow typography-eyebrow typography-site-deep-dive-eyebrow">Action mode</p>
                                        <p class="typography-site-header-2">
                                            Shaky shots, <br/>stable video.
                                        </p>

                                        <p>
                                            Whether you’re filming from an off-road SUV or running alongside your subject, use Action mode for <strong>smooth handheld videos</strong>
                                            .
                                        </p>
                                        <p>
                                            Just turn it on before you shoot to automatically get steady shots — <strong>no gimbal required</strong>
                                            .

                                                , so you don’t have to tap to see your favorite widgets like Weather, Calendar, or Lunar Phase.

                                                iPhone 
                                                <strong>
                                                    shows you where <br class="ls"/>to point to maintain your connection
                                                </strong>
                                                . <br class="medium"/>
                                                You must be outdoors with a <br class="medium"/>
                                                clear <br class="large"/>
                                                view <br class="small"/>
                                                of the sky — and <br class="large"/>
                                                avoid obstructions such as &nbsp;mountains and <br class="large"/>heavy foliage.
                                            </p>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="dd-layout dd-layout-device-img-v-txt dd-large-8 dd-medium-11 dd-small-20 dd-content-questions">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="dd-large-4 dd-medium-5 dd-small-8">
                                            <div class="vertical-picture vertical-picture-key-features-features-esos-deep-dive-dd-emergency-questions" data-vertical-picture>

                                                    <picture class="key-features-features-esos-deep-dive-dd-emergency-questions image">

                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="copy dd-large-offset-1 dd-large-3 dd-medium-5 dd-small-offset-2 dd-small-10 typography-site-body-copy">
                                            <p>
                                                Since every second <br class="ls"/>
                                                counts, 
                                                <strong>
                                                    iPhone front-loads <br class="small"/>a few questions to assess your situation
                                                </strong>
                                                — just tap <br class="ls"/>to &nbsp;respond.
                                            </p>
                                            <p>
                                                <strong>
                                                    Satellites are moving targets <br class="medium"/>with low bandwidth
                                                </strong>
                                                , so it can <br class="medium"/>
                                                take minutes for messages to <br class="medium"/>get through.
                                            </p>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                    <div class="headline dd-large-6 dd-medium-8 dd-small-12 dd-small-offset-1">
                                        <p class="eyebrow typography-eyebrow typography-site-deep-dive-eyebrow">Crash Detection</p>
                                        <p class="typography-site-header-2">In a severe car crash, iPhone calls for help when you &nbsp;can’t.</p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="dd-layout dd-layout-txt-device-img-v dd-large-8 dd-medium-11 dd-small-20 dd-content-device">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="copy dd-large-3 dd-medium-5 dd-small-10 typography-site-body-copy">
                                            <p>
                                                iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro 
                                                <strong>
                                                    can detect a <br class="small"/>
                                                    severe <br class="medium"/>car crash
                                                </strong>
                                                , then <br class="ls"/>
                                                call 911 and notify your emergency contacts.
                                                <sup class="footnote footnote-number">
                                                    <a href="#footnote-8" aria-label="Footnote 6" data-modal-close>6</a>
                                                </sup>
                                            </p>
                                            <p>
                                                <strong>Hardware sensors and advanced motion algorithms</strong>
                                                identify signs of a crash — including sudden changes <br class="ls"/>
                                                in speed, direction, and <br class="small"/>cabin pressure.
                                            </p>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="dd-large-4 dd-large-offset-1 dd-medium-5 dd-small-offset-2 dd-small-8">

                    . ACMI is not available for purchases made online at special storefronts. The last month’s payment for each product will be the product’s purchase price, less all other payments at the monthly payment amount.

            <ol>
                <li id="footnote-3">Trade-in values will vary based on the condition, year, and configuration of your eligible trade &#x2011;in device. Not all devices are eligible for credit. You must be at least 18 years old to be eligible to trade in for credit or for an Apple Gift Card. Trade &#x2011;in value may be applied toward qualifying new device purchase, or added to an Apple Gift Card. Actual value awarded is based on receipt of a qualifying device matching the description provided when estimate was made. Sales tax may be assessed on full value of a new device purchase. In &#x2011;store trade &#x2011;in requires presentation of a valid photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Offer may not be available in all stores, and may vary between in &#x2011;store and online trade &#x2011;in. Some stores may have additional requirements. Apple or its trade &#x2011;in partners reserve the right to refuse or limit quantity of any trade &#x2011;in transaction for any reason. More details are available from Apple’s trade &#x2011;in partner for trade &#x2011;in and recycling of eligible devices. Restrictions and limitations may apply.</li>
                <li id="footnote-4">
                    All battery claims depend on network configuration and many other factors; actual results will vary. Battery has limited recharge cycles and may eventually need to be replaced. Battery life and charge cycles vary by use and settings. See <a href="https://www.apple.com/batteries/">apple.com/batteries</a>
                    and <a href="https://www.apple.com/iphone/battery.html">apple.com/iphone/battery.html</a>
                    for more information.
                </li>
                <li id="footnote-5">Accessories sold separately.</li>
                <li id="footnote-6">iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro and iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro &nbsp;Max are splash, water, and dust resistant and were tested under controlled laboratory conditions with a rating of IP68 under IEC standard 60529 (maximum depth of 6 meters up to 30 minutes). Splash, water, and dust resistance are not permanent conditions. Resistance might decrease as a result of normal wear. Do not attempt to charge a wet iPhone; refer to the user guide for cleaning and drying instructions. Liquid damage not covered under warranty.</li>
                <li id="footnote-7">
                    Service is included for free for two years with the activation of any iPhone &nbsp;14 model. Connection and response times vary based on location, site conditions, and other factors. See <a href="https://support.apple.com/kb/HT213426">https://support.apple.com/kb/HT213426</a>
                    for more information.
                </li>
                <li id="footnote-8">iPhone &nbsp;14 and iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro can detect a severe car crash and call for help. Requires a cellular connection or Wi-Fi calling.</li>
                <li id="footnote-9">The display has rounded corners that follow a beautiful curved design, and these corners are within a standard rectangle. When measured as a standard rectangular shape, the screen is 5.42 &nbsp;inches (iPhone &nbsp;13 &nbsp;mini), 6.06 &nbsp;inches (iPhone &nbsp;14, iPhone &nbsp;13), 6.12 &nbsp;inches (iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro), 6.68 &nbsp;inches (iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Plus), or 6.69 &nbsp;inches (iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro &nbsp;Max) diagonally. Actual viewable area is less.</li>
                <li id="footnote-10" data-toggle-footnote="carriers">
                    <span class="bold">AT &T Special Deal:</span>
                    Monthly price reflects net monthly payment, after application of AT &T trade &#8209;in credit applied over 36 months with purchase of an iPhone 14 Pro, iPhone 14 Pro Max, iPhone 14, or iPhone 14 Plus and trade &#8209;in of eligible smartphone. Receive credit with purchase of an iPhone 14 Pro or iPhone 14 Pro Max of either $1000, $700, or $350 (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone). Receive credit with purchase of an iPhone 14 or iPhone 14 Plus of either $700 or $350 (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone). Max bill credits will not exceed the cost of the device. Requires upgrade of an existing line or activation of a new line and purchase of a new iPhone 14, iPhone 14 Plus, iPhone 14 Pro, or iPhone 14 Pro Max on qualifying 36 month 0% APR installment plan, subject to carrier credit qualification. AT &T Installment Plan with Next Up is not eligible for this promotion. $0 down for well qualified customers only, or down payment may be required and depends on a variety of factors. Tax on full retail price due at sale. Requires activation on eligible unlimited plan. If you cancel eligible wireless service, credits will stop and you will owe the remaining device balance. Activation/Upgrade Fee: $35. Trade in device may not be on existing installment plan. Bill credits are applied as a monthly credit over the 36 month installment plan. Credits start within 3 bills. Will receive catchup credits once credits start. Wireless line must be on an installment agreement, active, and in good standing for 30 days to qualify. Installment agreement starts when device is shipped. To get all credits, device must remain on agreement for entire term and you must keep eligible service on device for entire installment term. Limited time offer; subject to change. Limits: one trade &#8209;in per qualifying purchase and one credit per line. May not be combinable with other offers, discounts, or credits. Purchase, financing, other limits, and restrictions apply. Price for iPhone 14 and iPhone 14 Plus includes $30 AT &T connectivity discount. Activation required.
<br/>
                    <br/>
                    <span class="bold">T &#8209;Mobile Special Deal:</span>
                    Monthly price reflects net monthly payment, after application of T &#8209;Mobile trade &#8209;in credit applied over 24 months with purchase of an iPhone 14 Pro, iPhone 14 Pro Max, iPhone 14, or iPhone 14 Plus and trade &#8209;in of eligible smartphone. Receive credit with purchase of an iPhone 14, iPhone 14 Plus, iPhone 14 Pro, or iPhone 14 Pro Max of $350 or $175 for customers on a Magenta® MAX plan (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone); or $200 or $100 for customers on a non-Magenta® MAX plan except Select Choice, Base Essentials, and Value Essentials (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone). Max bill credits will not exceed the cost of the device. Credit comprised of (i) Apple instant trade &#8209;in credit at checkout and (ii) T &#8209;Mobile monthly bill credits applied over 24 months. Customer must remain in the T &#8209;Mobile Equipment Installment Program and on eligible data plan for 24 months and remain in good standing to receive the full benefit of the bill credits; allow 2 bill cycles from valid submission and validation of trade &#8209;in. Tax on pre-credit price due at sale. Limited-time offer; subject to change. Qualifying credit, data plan, and trade &#8209;in in good condition required. Max 4 promotional offers on any iPhone per account. May not be combinable with some offers or discounts. Price for iPhone 14 and iPhone 14 Plus includes $30 T &#8209;Mobile connectivity discount. Activation required. Contact T &#8209;Mobile before cancelling service to continue remaining bill credits on current device, or credits stop &balance on required finance agreement is due.
<br/>
                    <br/>
                    <span class="bold">Verizon Special Deal:</span>
                    Monthly price reflects net monthly payment, after application of Verizon trade &#8209;in credit applied over 36 months with purchase of an iPhone 14 Pro, iPhone 14 Pro Max, iPhone 14, or iPhone 14 Plus with credit of $440 or $220 for customers on an Unlimited Plus, One Unlimited, 5G Get More, 5G Do More, or 5G Play More plan (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone); or $220 or $100 for customers on a Welcome Unlimited or 5G Start plan (based upon the model and condition of your trade &#8209;in smartphone). Credit comprised of (i) Apple instant trade &#8209;in credit at checkout and (ii) Verizon monthly bill credits applied over 36 months. Customer must remain in the Verizon Device Payment Program for 36 months to receive the full benefit of the Verizon bill credits. Bill credits may take 1 &#8209;2 bill cycles to appear. If it takes two cycles for bill credits to appear, you’ll see the credit for the first cycle on your second bill in addition to that month’s credit. Requires purchase and activation of a new iPhone 14, iPhone 14 Plus, iPhone 14 Pro, or iPhone 14 Pro Max with the Verizon Device Payment Program at 0% APR for 36 months, subject to carrier credit qualification, and iPhone availability and limits. Taxes and shipping not included in monthly price. Sales tax may be assessed on full value of new iPhone. Requires eligible unlimited service plan. Requires trade &#8209;in of eligible device in eligible condition. Must be at least 18 to trade &#8209;in. Apple or its trade &#8209;in partners reserve the right to refuse or limit any trade &#8209;in transaction for any reason. In &#8209;store trade &#8209;in requires presentation of a valid, government &#8209;issued photo ID (local law may require saving this information). In &#8209;store promotion availability subject to local law; speak to a Specialist to learn more. Limited &#8209;time offer; subject to change. Additional terms from Apple, Verizon, and Apple’s trade &#8209;in partners may apply. Price for iPhone 14 and iPhone 14 Plus includes $30 Verizon connectivity discount. Activation required.
                </li>
                <li id="footnote-11">
                    Data plan required. 5G is available in select markets and through select carriers. Speeds vary based on site conditions and carrier. For details on 5G support, contact your carrier and see <a href="https://www.apple.com/iphone/cellular/">apple.com/iphone/cellular</a>
                    .
                </li>
                <li id="footnote-12">Program available for iPhone &nbsp;14 and iPhone &nbsp;14 &nbsp;Pro. Available to qualified customers with a credit check and eligible U.S. credit or debit card. Requires a 24 &#x2011;month installment loan with a 0% APR from Citizens Bank, N.A. (subject to any interest, fees, or other costs payable to the card issuer), purchase of AppleCare+ for iPhone, and iPhone activation with one of these national carriers: AT &amp;T, Verizon, or T &#x2011;Mobile. Sales tax and any applicable fees due at time of purchase. Full terms apply.</li>
            </ol>
            <ul>
                <li>
                    Some features may not be available for all countries or all areas. <a href="https://www.apple.com/ios/feature-availability/">View complete list</a>
                    .
                </li>
                <li data-toggle-footnote="acmi">
                    <small>†</small>
                    Apple Card Monthly Installments (ACMI) is a 0% APR payment option available only in the U.S. to select at checkout for certain Apple products purchased at Apple Store locations, <a href="https://www.apple.com/">apple.com</a>
                    , the Apple Store app, or by calling 1-800-MY-APPLE and is subject to credit approval and credit limit. See <a href="https://support.apple.com/kb/HT211204">support.apple.com/kb/HT211204</a>
                    for more information about eligible products. Variable APRs for Apple Card other than ACMI range from 15.74% to 26.74% based on creditworthiness. Rates as of April 1, 2023.
 If you choose the pay &#8209;in &#8209;full or one &#8209;time &#8209;payment option for an ACMI &#8209;eligible purchase instead of choosing ACMI as the payment option at checkout, that purchase will be subject to the variable APR assigned to your Apple Card. Taxes and shipping are not included in ACMI and are subject to your card’s variable APR. See the <a href="https://www.goldmansachs.com/terms-and-conditions/Apple-Card-Customer-Agreement.pdf" rel="nofollow">Apple Card Customer Agreement</a>
                    for more information. ACMI is not available for purchases made online at the following special stores: Apple Employee Purchase Plan; participating corporate Employee Purchase Programs; Apple at Work for small businesses; Government, and Veterans and Military Purchase Programs, or on refurbished devices. iPhone activation required on iPhone purchases made at an Apple Store with one of these national carriers: AT &T , Verizon, or T &#8209;Mobile.
                </li>
                <li data-toggle-footnote="acmi">
                    <p>To access and use all the features of Apple &nbsp;Card, you must add Apple &nbsp;Card to Wallet on an iPhone or iPad with the latest version of iOS or iPadOS. Update to the latest version by going to Settings &gt;General &gt;Software Update. Tap Download and Install.</p>
                    <p>Available for qualifying applicants in the United States.</p>
                    <p>Apple &nbsp;Card is issued by Goldman Sachs Bank USA, Salt Lake City Branch.</p>
                    <p>If you reside in the U.S. territories, please call Goldman Sachs at 877‑255‑5923 with questions about Apple &nbsp;Card.</p>
                </li>
            </ul>
        </section>
